Func NUIANHDAO()
	If Not $g_bComboSent Then
		_SendComboOnce()
	EndIf
	GUICtrlSetData($CRACK, "35")
_NUIANHDAO()  ;Checkpoint 1784
	Local $start = TimerInit()
	While TimerDiff($start) < 1
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET1, "1080806214")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET2, "3227479501")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET3, "1075104972")
	WEnd
